<p>(c) 110</p>
<p>(d) 1001</p>
<ol start="5">
<li><span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>11011</mn><msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">_</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">_</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">_</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">_</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">_</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(11011)_2 = (\_\_\_\_\_)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord">11011</span><span class="mclose"><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3011em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">2</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.06em; vertical-align: -0.31em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">_____</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span></li>
</ol>
<p>(a) <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>33</mn><msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mn>6</mn></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(33)_6</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord">33</span><span class="mclose"><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3011em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">6</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>(b) <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>17</mn><msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mn>8</mn></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(17)_8</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord">17</span><span class="mclose"><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3011em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">8</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>(c) <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>25</mn><msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mn>8</mn></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(25)_8</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord">25</span><span class="mclose"><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3011em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">8</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>(d) <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>28</mn><msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mn>8</mn></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(28)_8</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord">28</span><span class="mclose"><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3011em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">8</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<ol start="6">
<li>The 2's complement of 1100110 is ________</li>
</ol>
<p>(a) 0011001</p>
<p>(b) 0011010</p>
<p>(c) 1100001</p>
<p>(d) 1100010</p>
<ol start="7">
<li>The BCD representation of decimal 10 is ________</li>
</ol>
<p>(a) 00001010</p>
<p>(b) 00001001</p>
<p>(c) 00010000</p>
<p>(d) 10100000</p>
<ol start="8">
<li>The binary equivalent of <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>A</mi><mn>5</mn><msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mn>16</mn></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(A5)_{16}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span><span class="mord">5</span><span class="mclose"><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3011em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">16</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> is ________</li>
</ol>
<p>(a) 00100111</p>
<p>(b) 00100101</p>
<p>(c) 10100101</p>

<p>Communication Systems</p>
<ol start="13">
<li>
<p>The digital systems usually operate on ________ system.
(a) binary
(b) decimal
(c) octal
(d) hexadecimal</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>The binary system uses powers of ________ for positional values.
(a) 2
(b) 10
(c) 8
(d) 16</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>The number <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mn>1000</mn><mn>2</mn></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">1000_{2}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.7944em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord">100</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">0</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3011em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">2</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> is equivalent to decimal number
(a) one thousand
(b) eight
(c) four
(d) sixteen</p>

<li>
<p>The binary addition <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mn>1</mn><mo>+</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>+</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">1+1+1</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.7278em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.7278em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6444em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span></span></span></span></span> gives

(b) 10
(c) 110
(d) 11</p>
</li>
<li>

(d) 0001</p>

<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="iii-numerical-problems">III. Numerical Problems<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#iii-numerical-problems" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ol>
<li>A 500 W, 100 KHz carrier is modulated to a depth of  <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mn>60</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">%</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">60\%</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8056em; vertical-align: -0.0556em;"></span><span class="mord">60%</span></span></span></span></span>  by modulating signal frequency of 1 KHz. Calculate the total power transmitted. What are the sideband components of the AM wave? (VTU Jan 2010)</li>
<li>A carrier of 750 W, 1 MHz is amplitude modulated by sinusoidal signal of 2 KHz to a depth of  <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mn>50</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">%</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">50\%</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8056em; vertical-align: -0.0556em;"></span><span class="mord">50%</span></span></span></span></span> . Calculate bandwidth, power in each side band and total power transmitted. (VTU Jan 2008)</li>
<li>A carrier of 500 W, 1 MHz is amplitude modulated by sinusoidal signal of 1 KHz to a depth of  <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mn>60</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">%</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">60\%</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8056em; vertical-align: -0.0556em;"></span><span class="mord">60%</span></span></span></span></span> . Calculate bandwidth, power in each side band and total power transmitted. (VTU Jan 2007)</li>
<li>For an AM, amplitude of modulating signal is  <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mn>0.5</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">V</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">0.5\mathrm{V}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord">0.5</span><span class="mord mathrm" style="margin-right: 0.01389em;">V</span></span></span></span></span>  and carrier amplitude is  <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mn>1</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">V</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">1\mathrm{V}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mord mathrm" style="margin-right: 0.01389em;">V</span></span></span></span></span> . Find modulation index. (VTU Jan 2007)</li>
<li>A carrier of 500 W, 100 KHz is amplitude modulated by sinusoidal signal of 1 KHz to a depth of  <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mn>60</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">%</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">60\%</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8056em; vertical-align: -0.0556em;"></span><span class="mord">60%</span></span></span></span></span> . Calculate bandwidth, power in each side band and total power transmitted. (VTU Jan 2010)</li>
<li>Convert the following binary numbers to decimal numbers.
(i) 1101
(ii) 10001
(iii) 10101.</li>

<p>Communication Systems</p>
<ol start="7">
<li>
<p>(i) Convert <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>10110011010</mn><msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mn>2</mn></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(10110011010)_2</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord">10110011010</span><span class="mclose"><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3011em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">2</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> into octal, decimal and hexadecimal; (ii) Subtract using 2's complement <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>15</mn><mo>−</mo><mn>7</mn><msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mn>10</mn></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(15 - 7)_{10}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; </li>
